  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 分布式优化算法在多机器人系统中具有重要应用，但理论研究与实际测试存在差距，需要一种高效、低成本、可比对不同模型与真实硬件的验证方法。

Method: 采用SPMD（单程序多数据）并行范式，在单台计算机上，每个核心分别运行相同算法，通过本地状态和邻居通信实现分布式控制。以四架四旋翼机器人位置交换任务为例，运用非合作博弈分布式算法，比较了点质量模型、高保真四旋翼模型和真实硬件测试床的计算与轨迹数据。

Result: 该框架在不同动力学层次下均可运行；仿真与实验数据表明框架能有效比较算法性能，实现算法快速原型和低成本实验。

Conclusion: 本框架简单易用、成本低，有助于分布式控制算法从理论到实践的验证和推广。

Abstract: This paper presents a prototyping framework for distributed control of multi-robot systems, aimed at bridging theory and practical testing of distributed optimization algorithms. Using the Single Program, Multiple Data (SPMD) paradigm, the framework emulates distributed control on a single computer, with each core running the same algorithm using local states and neighbour-to-neighbour communication. We demonstrate the framework on a four-quadrotor position-swapping task using a non-cooperative game-theoretic distributed algorithm. Computational time and trajectory data are compared across the supported dynamics levels: a point-mass model, a high-fidelity quadrotor model, and an experimental hardware testbed using Crazyflie quadcopters. The results show that the framework provides a low-cost and accessible approach for validating distributed algorithms.

</details>


### [208] [SOCC-ICP: Semantics-Assisted Odometry based on Occupancy Grids and ICP](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15074)
*Johannes Scherer,Sebastian Hirt,Henri Meeß*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 提出SOCC-ICP框架，实现了同时进行语义占据网格构建和激光雷达扫描配准，提高自主系统在新环境中的位姿估计可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有激光雷达里程计使用的地图（如点云、NDT等）与机器人常用于下游任务（如运动规划）的语义占据网格分离，导致冗余和信息利用不充分。需要一种能够同时支持高精度定位和为下游应用直接提供地图的方法。

Method: 提出SOCC-ICP框架，将几何与语义统计编码于网格体素中，根据局部平面性自适应地选择ICP配准策略（点到点或点到面），并利用射线投影自然而然地过滤动态物体。框架支持集成语义信息以提升构建、下采样与关联权重的精度。

Result: 在多种评测环境中，SOCC-ICP获得了与最先进方法相当的性能，并在几何退化且无语义标签时依然表现出鲁棒性。如有语义标签，准确率进一步提升。

Conclusion: SOCC-ICP通过将里程计与语义占据网格统一，消除了多余的地图结构，直接为机器人下游应用提供高效适用的地图。

Abstract: Reliable pose estimation in previously unseen environments is a fundamental capability of autonomous systems. Existing LiDAR odometry methods typically employ point-, surfel-, or NDT-based map representations, which are distinct from the semantic occupancy grids commonly used for downstream tasks such as motion planning. We introduce SOCC-ICP, a semantics-assisted odometry framework that jointly performs Semantic OCCupancy grid mapping and LiDAR scan alignment. Each map voxel encodes geometric and semantic statistics, enabling adaptive point-to-point or point-to-plane ICP based on local planarity. Further, the occupancy grid naturally filters dynamic objects through raycasting-based free-space updates. Across diverse evaluation scenarios, SOCC-ICP achieves performance competitive with state-of-the-art LiDAR odometry and remains robust in geometrically degenerate environments, even in the absence of semantic cues. When semantic labels are available, integrating them into map construction, downsampling, and correspondence weighting yields further accuracy gains. By unifying odometry and semantic occupancy grid mapping within a single representation, SOCC-ICP eliminates redundant map structures and directly provides a map suitable for downstream robotic applications.

### [209] [CLOVER: Closed-Loop Value Estimation \& Ranking for End-to-End Autonomous Driving Planning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15120)
*Sining Ang,Yuguang Yang,Canyu Chen,Yan Wang*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: CLOVER提出了一种新的端到端自动驾驶规划框架，通过多样性轨迹生成与分数打分，实现更优的路径选择，突破了传统模仿单一路径的局限，并在多个基准上取得了新SOTA。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有端到端自动驾驶方法通常仿真单一演示轨迹，但实际评测更关注安全、舒适等多指标，因此训练与评测存在偏差，影响规划器性能。特别是候选轨迹集的覆盖度和排序能力会直接影响规划效果。

Method: CLOVER采用'生成器-评分器'结构，生成器产多样化轨迹候选，评分器对每条轨迹的各项规划指标打分排序。为提升生成器，不再只模仿单一专家轨迹，而是用过滤后的伪专家轨迹进行集合级监督，并通过保守的闭环自蒸馏调整生成器和评分器，保证优化稳定和高效。

Result: 在NAVSIM数据集上，CLOVER获94.5 PDMS和90.4 EPDMS，为新SOTA；在NavHard分支与最强结果持平；在nuScenes公开评测上，CLOVER L2误差和碰撞率均最低。

Conclusion: CLOVER有效解决了端到端自动驾驶训练与评测的偏差，通过生成-评分协调，提升了候选轨迹质量与最终规划表现，在多个评测基准上达到或超过现有最佳水平。

Abstract: End-to-end autonomous driving planners are commonly trained by imitating a single logged trajectory, yet evaluated by rule-based planning metrics that measure safety, feasibility, progress, and comfort. This creates a training--evaluation mismatch: trajectories close to the logged path may violate planning rules, while alternatives farther from the demonstration can remain valid and high-scoring. The mismatch is especially limiting for proposal-selection planners, whose performance depends on candidate-set coverage and scorer ranking quality. We propose CLOVER, a Closed-LOop Value Estimation and Ranking framework for end-to-end autonomous driving planning. CLOVER follows a lightweight generator--scorer formulation: a generator produces diverse candidate trajectories, and a scorer predicts planning-metric sub-scores to rank them at inference time. To expand proposal support beyond single-trajectory imitation, CLOVER constructs evaluator-filtered pseudo-expert trajectories and trains the generator with set-level coverage supervision. It then performs conservative closed-loop self-distillation: the scorer is fitted to true evaluator sub-scores on generated proposals, while the generator is refined toward teacher-selected top-$k$ and vector-Pareto targets with stability regularization. We analyze when an imperfect scorer can improve the generator, showing that scorer-mediated refinement is reliable when scorer-selected targets are enriched under the true evaluator and updates remain conservative. On NAVSIM, CLOVER achieves 94.5 PDMS and 90.4 EPDMS, establishing a new state of the art. On the more challenging NavHard split, it obtains 48.3 EPDMS, matching the strongest reported result. On supplementary nuScenes open-loop evaluation, CLOVER achieves the lowest L2 error and collision rate among compared methods. Code data will be released at https://github.com/WilliamXuanYu/CLOVER.

</details>


### [210] [CoCo-InEKF: State Estimation with Learned Contact Covariances in Dynamic, Contact-Rich Scenarios](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15122)
*Michael Baumgartner,David Müller,Agon Serifi,Ruben Grandia,Espen Knoop,Markus Gross,Moritz Bächer*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种适用于动态多变和复杂接触场景下腿式机器人运动的鲁棒状态估计算法CoCo-InEKF，通过持续的接触速度协方差建模，提高了速度估算的精度和一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的状态估计方法只依赖于二值化的接触状态，无法细致表达部分接触或方向滑移等复杂接触情况，导致在高度动态和接触丰富的运动任务中估算能力有限。

Method: 提出了CoCo-InEKF方法，其核心是利用可学习的接触速度协方差替代二元接触表示。通过端到端训练的小型神经网络，根据状态误差预测每个预设接触点的协方差，无需人工标注接触标签。同时，提出了自动化的接触候选点选择流程，且对点位选择具有不敏感性。

Result: 在仿真与真实二足机器人实验中，该方法在速度估算的准确性与计算效率之间达到了更优平衡，并显著提升了滤波器的一致性，超越了多种对比基线方法。

Conclusion: CoCo-InEKF方法无需启发式标签，能在各种复杂动态任务（如跳舞或复杂地面交互）下表现出高鲁棒性与精度，对未来腿式机器人在多变环境下的可靠控制具有重要意义。

Abstract: Robust state estimation for highly dynamic motion of legged robots remains challenging, especially in dynamic, contact-rich scenarios. Traditional approaches often rely on binary contact states that fail to capture the nuances of partial contact or directional slippage. This paper presents CoCo-InEKF, a differentiable invariant extended Kalman filter that utilizes continuous contact velocity covariances instead of binary contact states. These learned covariances allow the method to dynamically modulate contact confidence, accounting for more nuanced conditions ranging from firm contact to directional slippage or no contact. To predict these covariances for a set of predefined contact candidate points, we employ a lightweight neural network trained end-to-end using a state-error loss. This approach eliminates the need for heuristic ground-truth contact labels. In addition, we propose an automated contact candidate selection procedure and demonstrate that our method is insensitive to their exact placement. Experiments on a bipedal robot demonstrate a superior accuracy-efficiency tradeoff for linear velocity estimation, as well as improved filter consistency compared to baseline methods. This enables the robust execution of challenging motions, including dancing and complex ground interactions -- both in simulation and in the real world.

</details>


### [211] [Pelican-Unified 1.0: A Unified Embodied Intelligence Model for Understanding, Reasoning, Imagination and Action](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15153)
*Yi Zhang,Yinda Chen,Che Liu,Zeyuan Ding,Jin Xu,Shilong Zou,Junwei Liao,Jiayu Hu,Xiancong Ren,Xiaopeng Zhang,Yechi Liu,Haoyuan Shi,Zecong Tang,Haosong Sun,Renwen Cui,Kuishu Wu,Wenhai Liu,Yang Xu,Yingji Zhang,Yidong Wang,Senkang Hu,Jinpeng Lu,Nga Teng Chan,Yechen Wu,Yong Dai,Jian Tang,Xiaozhu Ju*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: Pelican-Unified 1.0是第一个基于统一原则训练的具身基础模型，实现了理解、推理、想象和行动的统一。实验显示其在多项任务上表现优异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前多模态具身智能模型往往将理解、推理与行动等能力分为多个独立系统，模型间难以协同优化。作者希望通过统一架构，将这些能力集成进一个模型中，提高整体性能和泛化能力。

Method: 模型采用单一的视觉语言模型（VLM）作为统一的理解与推理模块，将场景、指令、视觉上下文与动作历史映射到共享语义空间。VLM自回归地产生思维链并输出隐状态，随后统一未来生成器（UFG）通过去噪过程生成未来视频与动作。所有损失直接作用于共享表征，实现多能力的协同优化。

Result: Pelican-Unified 1.0在三方面均表现突出：在8个VLM基准测试上得分64.7，位列同规模模型第一；WorldArena得分66.03，排名第一；RoboTwin得分93.5，为行动方法中第二高。

Conclusion: 统一范式不仅没有削弱专业能力，还将模型的理解、推理、想象和行动能力集于一体，实现了多项任务均衡且优异的性能。

Abstract: We present Pelican-Unified 1.0, the first embodied foundation model trained according to the principle of unification. Pelican-Unified 1.0 uses a single VLM as a unified understanding module, mapping scenes, instructions, visual contexts, and action histories into a shared semantic space. The same VLM also serves as a unified reasoning module, autoregressively producing task-, action-, and future-oriented chains of thought in a single forward pass and projecting the final hidden state into a dense latent variable. A Unified Future Generator (UFG) then conditions on this latent variable and jointly generates future videos and future actions through two modality-specific output heads within the same denoising process. The language, video, and action losses are all backpropagated into the shared representation, enabling the model to jointly optimize understanding, reasoning, imagination, and action during training, rather than training three isolated expert systems.
  Experiments demonstrate that unification does not imply compromise. With a single checkpoint, Pelican-Unified 1.0 achieves strong performance across all three capabilities: 64.7 on eight VLM benchmarks, the best among comparable-scale models; 66.03 on WorldArena, ranking first; and 93.5 on RoboTwin, the second-best average among compared action methods. These results show that the unified paradigm succeeds in preserving specialist strength while bringing understanding, reasoning, imagination, and action into one model.

</details>
